  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // 👉 Afficher uniquement sur les articles (single-post)
    if (!document.body.classList.contains('single-post')) {
      return;
    }

    function createSlug(text) {
      return text.toLowerCase()
        .replace(/[^\w\s-]/g, '')
        .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
        .trim();
    }
    
    const possibleContainers = [
      '.entry-content', 
      '.gb-container',
      'article.post',
      'main.site-main',
      '.inside-article'
    ];
    
    let articleContainer = null;
    for (const selector of possibleContainers) {
      const container = document.querySelector(selector);
      if (container) {
        const headings = container.querySelectorAll('h2');
        if (headings.length > 0) {
          articleContainer = container;
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    if (articleContainer) {
      const headings = articleContainer.querySelectorAll('h2');
      
      if (headings.length > 0) {
        const tocList = document.getElementById('toc-list');
        
        headings.forEach(function(heading) {
          if (heading.classList.contains('no-toc')) return;
          
          const headingText = heading.textContent.trim();
          if (!headingText) return;
          
          const slug = createSlug(headingText);
          if (!heading.id) {
            heading.id = slug;
          }
          
          const listItem = document.createElement('li');
          const bulletSpan = document.createElement('span');
          bulletSpan.className = 'toc-bullet';
          bulletSpan.textContent = '•';
          listItem.appendChild(bulletSpan);
          
          const link = document.createElement('a');
          link.href = '#' + heading.id;
          link.textContent = headingText;
          
          listItem.appendChild(link);
          tocList.appendChild(listItem);
        });
        
        const recipeCard = articleContainer.querySelector('.wp-block-wpzoom-recipe-card, .wprm-recipe-container, .tasty-recipes, .recipe-card, [id*="recipe-card"], [class*="recipe-card"]');
        
        if (recipeCard) {
          if (!recipeCard.id) {
            recipeCard.id = 'recipe-card';
          }
          
          const recipeListItem = document.createElement('li');
          const bulletSpan = document.createElement('span');
          bulletSpan.className = 'toc-bullet';
          bulletSpan.textContent = '•';
          recipeListItem.appendChild(bulletSpan);
          
          const recipeLink = document.createElement('a');
          recipeLink.href = '#' + recipeCard.id;
          
          const recipeIcon = document.createElement('span');
          recipeIcon.className = 'recipe-card-icon';
          recipeIcon.innerHTML = '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M3 2v7c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h4a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V2"></path><path d="M7 2v20"></path><path d="M21 15v4a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2v-4"></path><path d="M12 15V2"></path><path d="M17 15V2"></path><path d="M21 2v13"></path></svg>';
          
          recipeLink.appendChild(recipeIcon);
          recipeLink.appendChild(document.createTextNode('Recipe Card'));
          
          recipeListItem.appendChild(recipeLink);
          tocList.appendChild(recipeListItem);
        }
        
        const tocContainer = document.getElementById('auto-toc-container');
        const featuredImage = articleContainer.querySelector('.wp-post-image, .featured-image img, .post-thumbnail img');
        
        let insertAfter = null;
        
        if (featuredImage) {
          let imageContainer = featuredImage;
          while (imageContainer.parentElement && 
                 imageContainer.parentElement !== articleContainer && 
                 !['div', 'figure'].includes(imageContainer.parentElement.tagName.toLowerCase())) {
            imageContainer = imageContainer.parentElement;
          }
          insertAfter = imageContainer;
        } else {
          const possibleFeaturedContainers = articleContainer.querySelectorAll('figure, .featured-image, .post-thumbnail, .wp-block-image');
          if (possibleFeaturedContainers.length > 0) {
            insertAfter = possibleFeaturedContainers[0];
          } else {
            const paragraphs = articleContainer.querySelectorAll('p');
            if (paragraphs.length > 0) {
              insertAfter = paragraphs[0];
            } else {
              insertAfter = headings[0].previousElementSibling || articleContainer.firstChild;
            }
          }
        }
        
        if (insertAfter && insertAfter.parentNode) {
          insertAfter.parentNode.insertBefore(tocContainer, insertAfter.nextSibling);
          tocContainer.style.display = 'block';
          
          const tocHeader = document.querySelector('.toc-header');
          tocHeader.addEventListener('click', function() {
            tocContainer.classList.toggle('open');
          });
          
          const tocLinks = document.querySelectorAll('#toc-list a');
          tocLinks.forEach(link => {
            link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
              e.preventDefault();
              
              const targetId = this.getAttribute('href').substring(1);
              const targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId);
              
              if (targetElement) {
                const headerOffset = 80;
                const elementPosition = targetElement.getBoundingClientRect().top;
                const offsetPosition = elementPosition + window.pageYOffset - headerOffset;
                
                window.scrollTo({
                  top: offsetPosition,
                  behavior: 'smooth'
                });
              }
            });
          });
        }
      }
    }
  });
</script>
